[0m[35mlibs/stream-ui/developers/PR.md[0m
[0m[32m31[0m:It may often be the case, that you are implementing a feature with changes in styling ([`[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-css`](https://github.com/GetStream/[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-css)) or Stream Chat API client (`[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-js`). Those PRs may contain changes on which depends the functionality of the currently created PR in `[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-react`. In such case, you should include references to PRs in those repos as well (e.g. `Depends on https://github.com/GetStream/[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-css/issues/66`).

[0m[35mlibs/stream-ui/developers/RELEASE.md[0m
[0m[32m3[0m:The `[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-react` package follows semantic versioning and the release is to a big part automated by `semantic-release`. The utility automates:
[0m[32m6[0m:2. [GitHub release](https://github.com/GetStream/[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-react/releases) creation
[0m[32m16[0m:1. Convert the current latest branch to a version branch by creating a PR with adjusted `.releaserc.json`. Example PR: https://github.com/GetStream/[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-react/pull/2507
[0m[32m18[0m:2. Configure the `master` branch back from `prerelease` to `latest` and add a config for the next version branch also designated as `latest`. Example PR: https://github.com/GetStream/[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-react/pull/2506.
[0m[32m24[0m:1. make sure that all the new required features and bug fixes in peer dependency repositories `@stream-io/[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-css` and `[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-js` are released
[0m[32m25[0m:2. make sure that the peer dependencies `@stream-io/[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-css` and `[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-js` are installed at their latest version (see `package.json`, `yarn.lock`) (if applicable)
[0m[32m27[0m:4. navigate to ["Actions"](https://github.com/GetStream/[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-react/actions) and in the left bar select the "Release" workflow
[0m[32m34[0m:- `docs_env` (required) option offers two environment options to which the documentation will be pushed to via `GetStream/push-[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-docusaurus-action` - defaults to `staging`
[0m[32m38[0m:We maintain multiple demo applications developed with `[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-react`. With each new version of the package, the applications should have their dependencies upgraded explicitly in their `package.json`.

[0m[32m2633[0m:### âš ï¸ BREAKING CHANGES âš ï¸ - Please review our v6 [implementation guide](https://github.com/GetStream/[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-react/wiki) prior to upgrading.
[0m[32m2642[0m:**NOTE:** The `ChannelContext` no longer exists, so all old references to `useChannelContext()` or `useContext(ChannelContext)` need to be replaced with the relevant context above. A list of all data found within each new context can be found [here](https://github.com/GetStream/[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-react/wiki/Context-Overview-(v6.0.0)).
[0m[32m2646[0m:- We've added a handful of new features in this release, check out this [wiki](https://github.com/GetStream/[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-react/wiki/New-Features-(v.6.0.0)) for more details. New features include:
[0m[32m2653[0m:- The `Message` component now provides the `MessageContext` to its children. Reference this [guide](https://github.com/GetStream/[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-react/wiki/How-to-Guide-for-Building-a-Custom-Message-(v.6.0.0)) for instructions on creating a custom message UI component.
[0m[32m2654[0m:- The `MessageInput` component now provides the `MessageInputContext` to its children. Reference this [guide](https://github.com/GetStream/[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-react/wiki/How-to-Guide-for-Building-a-Custom-MessageInput-and-Customizing-the-Default-MessageInput-(v.6.0.0)) for instructions on creating a custom input UI component.

[0m[35mlibs/stream-ui/CONTRIBUTING.md[0m
[0m[32m1[0m:# Contributing to [0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-react
[0m[32m17[0m:Package `[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-react` has a peer dependency [[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-js](https://github.com/GetStream/[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-js) - a client library for interacting with the Stream Chat API (see the [API docs](https://getstream.io/chat/docs/javascript/?language=javascript)).
[0m[32m19[0m:### 2. Documentation for [0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-react
[0m[32m21[0m:The [[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-react](https://getstream.io/chat/docs/sdk/react/) documentation is held separately from the Stream Chat API docs. Besides documenting the component API, it provides examples of their use in various scenarios.
[0m[32m35[0m:Spotting imperfections and not keeping them to yourself is the first step to make this library better. We are very grateful for reports concerning imperfections in the source code or the [documentation](<(https://getstream.io/chat/docs/sdk/react/)>). Before filing an issue, please, review the list of [open issues](https://github.com/GetStream/[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-react/issues) first.
[0m[32m39[0m:You can report a source code bug by using the [Bug Report template](https://github.com/GetStream/[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-react/issues/new/choose). Make sure you include "steps to reproduce" section. Bug that cannot be reproduced cannot be solved.
[0m[32m45[0m:You can request a feature by submitting a [Feature request issue](https://github.com/GetStream/[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-react/issues/new?assignees=&labels=feature&template=feature_request.md&title=) in our repository. If you would like to implement the proposal, please state it in the issue. It will allow us to discuss the proposal and better coordinate the efforts. You can even ping us - mention `@GetStream/stream-react-developers ` in the issue.
[0m[32m51[0m:It is always good to get acquainted with the specifics of the package. For example the `[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-react` package has its peer dependencies (`[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-js`, `[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-css`), which you may need to tweak at the same time, while developing the feature for `[0m[1m[31mstream-chat[0m-react`. To get more into those specifics, please read [development guide](./developers/DEVELOPMENT.md).
